                   <div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft='{"tn":"K"}'>
                    <p>
                     The IJCU shares in mourning the death of Elie Wiesel. We rededicate ourselves through our Youth &amp; Prejudice: Reducing Hatred program to advancing the values and principles he so courageously and eloquently framed for the world, by learning from the Shoa how to shape a more humane, responsive, and mutually respectful community locally and globally. May his memory and his legacy stand forever as a blessing.
                    </p>

                   <div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft='{"tn":"K"}'>
                    <p>
                     We at IJCU are planning The Youth and Prejudice: Reducing Hatred Conference for High School students from the region. It  will take place Wednesday, November 18th and Thursday, November 19th. There are many roles for community facilitators, Muhlenberg College students, faculty and staff, and of course, those who tell their own or their family&#039;s Holocaust Survivor stories. Contact mlightwood&#064;muhlenberg.edu or comment here if you&#039;d like to participate this year.
                    </p>

It turned out that the wisdom of God in a mystery is about evidence (with the help of God written entitled; \u201cGood News! Salvation Comes! Saved by Grace Through Faith\u201d, \u201cThe TRUTH That Make You Free\u201d, and \u201cAn Open Letter To All Religious Communities\u201d).\n\n\nSo now the debate between believers and nonbelievers, ended. Bible truth has been proved. His prophecies were fulfilled precisely.\n\n\nWhen the Bible proves true, then all that speaks against the truth of the Bible, proved to be a lie.\n\n\n1 John 2:22 22 Who is a liar but he that denieth that Jesus is the Christ? He is antichrist, that denieth the Father and the Son.\n\n\nAll men should honour the Son.\n\n\nJohn 5:23 ; That all men should honour the Son, even as they honour the Father. He that honoureth not the Son honoureth not the Father which hath sent him.)\n\n\nHebrew 1:6 And again, when he bringeth in the firstbegotten into the world, he saith, And let all the angels of God worship him. \n\n\nJohn 14:6 Jesus saith unto him, I am the way, the truth, and the life: no man cometh unto the Father, but by me.\n\n\n1 John2:23 Whosoever denieth the Son, the same hath not the Father: he that acknowledgeth the Son hath the Father also.\n\n\nJohn 6:45 It is written in the prophets, And they shall be all taught of God. right paths.\n\n\nMathew 7:14 Because strait is the gate, and narrow is the way, which leadeth unto life, and few there be that find it. \n\n\nProverbs 14:12 There is a way which seemeth right unto a man, but the end thereof are the ways of death. \n\n\nIsaiah 55:8 For my thoughts are not your thoughts, neither are your ways my ways, saith the YHWH. 55:9 For as the heavens are higher than the earth, so are my ways higher than your ways, and my thoughts than your thoughts.  10 For as the rain cometh down, and the snow from heaven, and returneth not thither, but watereth the earth, and maketh it bring forth and bud, that it may give seed to the sower, and bread to the eater:  55:11 So shall my word be that goeth forth out of my mouth: it shall not return unto me void, but it shall accomplish that which I please, and it shall prosper in the thing whereto I sent it. \n\n\nPsalm 119:105 Thy word is a lamp unto my feet, and a light unto my path. \n\n\nHosea 14:9 Who is wise, and he
